<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неудачный.html>неудачно</a> (10059)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неудачный.html>неуда́чный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">neudáčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неудобный.html>неудо́бный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neudóbnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неудо́бнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неудо́бней</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">удо́бнейший</b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неудовлетворенный.html>неудовлетворённый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">neudovletvorjónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>dissatisfaction, discontent

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">неукло́нный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">neuklónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неуклонно.html>неукло́нно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neuklónno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>steadily, relentlessly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пустить.html>пу́стим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самотек.html>самотёк</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:процент.html>проце́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:реальный.html>реа́льных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:потенциальный.html>потенциа́льных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:алкоголик.html>алкого́ликов</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:неуклонно.html>неукло́нно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:расти.html>расти́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jésli my pústim vsjó éto na samotjók, to procént reálʹnyx i potɛnciálʹnyx alkogólikov búdet <b>neuklónno</b> rastí</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">If we let all this run its course, the percentage of actual and potential alcoholics will increase <b>steadily</b></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>steadfastly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">Саратовцы <a href = vnd.unilang:опускаться.html>опуска́ются</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:турнирный.html>турни́рной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:таблица.html>табли́це</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:медленно.html>ме́дленно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:неуклонно.html>неукло́нно</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Saratovcy opuskájutsja v turnírnoj tablíce médlenno, no <b>neuklónno</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The Saratov (FC) players are slowly but <b>surely</b> signing themselves off the league standings</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>progressively</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неуклюжий.html>неуклю́жий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">neukljúžij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>

</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">укроти́мый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukrotímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неукротимый.html>неукроти́мый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neukrotímyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неукроти́мее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неукроти́мей</b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уловимый.html>улови́мый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ulovímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неуловимый.html>неулови́мый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neulovímyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>elusive, difficult to catch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:неуловимый.html>неулови́м</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>neulovím</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is not to be caught</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>imperceptible, subtle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неуловимый.html>неулови́мый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:звук.html>звук</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neulovímyj</b> zvuk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">imperceptible sound</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неуловимый.html>неулови́мая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:разница.html>ра́зница</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neulovímaja</b> ráznica</i> ― <span class="e-translation">subtle/indefinable difference</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неумелый.html>неуме́лый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">neumélyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>

***неуместный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неуместный.html>неуме́стный</a> (9245)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уместный.html>уме́стный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uméstnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неуместный.html>неуме́стный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neuméstnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неуме́стнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неуме́стней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>misplaced, inappropriate, out of place, unsuitable, unfitting, irrelevant
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неуместный.html>неуме́стное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:замечание.html>замеча́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neuméstnoje</b> zamečánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">untimely remark</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>здесь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:неуместный.html>неуме́стно</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zdesʹ éto <b>neuméstno</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it is out of place here</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">неподоба́ющий</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nepodobájuščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:урожай.html>урожа́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">urožáj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неурожай.html>неурожа́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neurožáj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неурожай.html>неурожа́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неурожай.html>неурожа́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неурожай.html>неурожа́ев</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уста.html>уст</a>(а́ть)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ust(átʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́нный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неустанный.html>неуста́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neustánnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>constant, incessant, relentless</li>
<li>tireless</li></ol>

***неустойка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неустойка.html>неусто́йка</a> (29764)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устоять.html>устоя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ustojátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неустойка.html>неусто́йка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neustójka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неустойка.html>неусто́йки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неустойка.html>неусто́йки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неустойка.html>неусто́ек</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">неусто́ечный</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> penal damages, stipulated damages <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in a civil law system, the monetary penalty for nonfulfillment of a contractual obligation</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> failure</li></ol>
